**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Agentic Correctness: Implement Kubernetes Custom Resource Client

## Your Task

Write a Go file `crd_client.go` that implements a typed client for a custom resource `Widget` (group `example.com`, version `v1`). Your implementation must follow the patterns established in the Kubernetes client-go codebase: 1. Embed or use the `rest.Interface` client from `k8s.io/client-go/rest`. 2. Implement `Create`, `Get`, `List`, and `Delete` methods following the same parameter conventions as `k8s.io/client-go/kubernetes/typed/` clients. 3. Use proper `context.Context` propagation. Write your implementation to `/workspace/crd_client.go`. Also write `/workspace/answer.json` listing the client-go source files you referenced.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the org domain.

## Available Resources

No local repositories are pre-checked out.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
*(none — all repos available locally)*

## Output Format

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{
  "files": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go"}
  ],
  "symbols": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "SymbolName"}
  ],
  "chain": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "FunctionName"}
  ],
  "text": "Narrative explanation of your findings, citing repos and file paths."
}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

## Evaluation

Your answer will be scored on:
- **File recall and precision**: Did you find all relevant files?
- **Keyword presence**: Are required terms present in your explanation?

## Summary

I've implemented a complete Kubernetes Custom Resource (Widget) typed client following the established patterns in the client-go codebase.

### Created Files:

**1. `/workspace/crd_client.go`** - A full-featured typed client implementation for the Widget custom resource (API group: `example.com`, version: `v1`) that includes:

- **Resource Types**: Widget and WidgetList definitions with proper Kubernetes metadata (TypeMeta, ObjectMeta, ListMeta)
- **Client Interfaces**: WidgetsGetter and WidgetInterface with the required methods:
  - `Create(ctx context.Context, widget *Widget, opts metav1.CreateOptions) (*Widget, error)`
  - `Get(ctx context.Context, name string, opts metav1.GetOptions) (*Widget, error)`
  - `List(ctx context.Context, opts metav1.ListOptions) (*WidgetList, error)`
  - `Delete(ctx context.Context, name string, opts metav1.DeleteOptions) error`
- **Group-Level Client** (ExampleV1Client) with factory methods:
  - `NewForConfig()` - Creates client from rest.Config
  - `NewForConfigAndClient()` - Creates client with custom HTTP client
  - `NewForConfigOrDie()` - Creates client or panics
  - `New()` - Creates client from rest.Interface
- **REST Implementation**: Uses `rest.Interface` to build request chains with proper namespace handling, resource names, and context propagation
- **Configuration Handling**: Proper scheme setup with GroupVersion, APIPath, and codec configuration

`json:\",inline\"`\n\tmetav1.ObjectMeta `json:\"metadata,omitempty\"`\n\tSpec              WidgetSpec   `json:\"spec,omitempty\"`\n\tStatus            WidgetStatus `json:\"status,omitempty\"`\n}\n\n// `json:\"replicas,omitempty\"`\n}\n\n// WidgetStatus defines the observed state of a Widget\ntype WidgetStatus struct {\n\tReady    bool   `json:\"ready,omitempty\"`\n\tMessage  string `json:\"message,omitempty\"`\n\tReplicas int32  `json:\"replicas,omitempty\"`\n}\n\n// WidgetList is a list of Widget objects\ntype WidgetList struct {\n\tmetav1.TypeMeta (*WidgetList, error)\n\tDelete(ctx context.Context, name string, opts metav1.DeleteOptions) error\n}\n\n// ExampleV1Client is used to interact with features provided by the example.com group\ntype ExampleV1Client struct {\n\trestClient rest.Interface\n}\n\n// NewForConfig creates a new ExampleV1Client for the given config.\n// NewForConfig is equivalent to NewForConfigAndClient(c, httpClient),\n// where httpClient was generated with rest.HTTPClientFor(c).\nfunc NewForConfig(c *rest.Config) (*ExampleV1Client, error) {\n\tconfig := *c\n\tif err := setConfigDefaults(&config); err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\thttpClient, err := rest.HTTPClientFor(&config)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\treturn NewForConfigAndClient(&config, httpClient)\n}\n\n// NewForConfigAndClient creates a new ExampleV1Client for the given config and http client.\n// Note the http client provided takes precedence over the configured transport values.\nfunc NewForConfigAndClient(c *rest.Config, h *http.Client) (*ExampleV1Client, error) {\n\tconfig := *c\n\tif err := setConfigDefaults(&config); err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\tclient, err := rest.RESTClientForConfigAndClient(&config, h)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\treturn &ExampleV1Client{client}, nil\n}\n\n// NewForConfigOrDie creates a new ExampleV1Client for the given config and\n// panics if there is an error in the config.\nfunc NewForConfigOrDie(c *rest.Config) *ExampleV1Client {\n\tclient, err := NewForConfig(c)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tpanic(err)\n\t}\n\treturn client\n}\n\n// New creates a new ExampleV1Client for the given RESTClient.\nfunc New(c rest.Interface) *ExampleV1Client {\n\treturn &ExampleV1Client{c}\n}\n\n// Widgets returns a WidgetInterface for the given namespace\nfunc (c *ExampleV1Client) Widgets(namespace string) WidgetInterface {\n\treturn newWidgets(c, namespace)\n}\n\n// RESTClient returns a setConfigDefaults(config *rest.Config) error {\n\tgv := schema.GroupVersion{Group: \"example.com\", Version: \"v1\"}\n\tconfig.GroupVersion = &gv\n\tconfig.APIPath = \"/apis\"\n\n\t// Create a scheme &Widget{})\n\tscheme.AddKnownTypeWithName(gv.WithKind(\"WidgetList\"), &WidgetList{})\n\n\t// Set up the serializer with the scheme\n\tconfig.NegotiatedSerializer = rest.CodecFactoryForGeneratedClient(scheme, runtime.NewCodecFactory(scheme)).WithoutConversion()\n\n\tif config.UserAgent == \"\" {\n\t\tconfig.UserAgent = rest.DefaultKubernetesUserAgent()\n\t}\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// widgets implements WidgetInterface\ntype widgets struct {\n\tclient    rest.Interface\n\tnamespace string\n}\n\n// newWidgets returns a // Widget is a custom resource definition (CRD) for the example.com API group, v1 version
// This is a minimal definition for demonstration purposes
type Widget struct {
	metav1.TypeMeta   `json:",inline"`
	metav1.ObjectMeta `json:"metadata,omitempty"`
	Spec              WidgetSpec   `json:"spec,omitempty"`
	Status            WidgetStatus `json:"status,omitempty"`
}

// WidgetSpec defines the desired state of a Widget
type WidgetSpec struct {
	Size     string `json:"size,omitempty"`
	Color    string `json:"color,omitempty"`
	Replicas *int32 `json:"replicas,omitempty"`
}

// WidgetStatus defines the observed state of a Widget
type WidgetStatus struct {
	Ready    bool   `json:"ready,omitempty"`
	Message  string `json:"message,omitempty"`
	Replicas int32  `json:"replicas,omitempty"`
}

// WidgetList is a list of Widget objects
type WidgetList struct {
	metav1.TypeMeta `json:",inline"`
	metav1.ListMeta `json:"metadata,omitempty"`
	Items           []Widget `json:"items"`
}

// ExampleV1Client is used to interact with features provided by the example.com group
type ExampleV1Client struct {
	restClient rest.Interface
}

// NewForConfig creates a new ExampleV1Client for the given config
func NewForConfig(c *rest.Config) (*ExampleV1Client, error) {
	config := *c
	if err := setConfigDefaults(&config); err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}
	client, err := rest.RESTClientFor(&config)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}
	return &ExampleV1Client{client}, nil
}

// New creates a new ExampleV1Client for the given RESTClient
func New(c rest.Interface) *ExampleV1Client {
	return &ExampleV1Client{c}
}
After
// ExampleV1Client is used to interact with features provided by the example.com group
type ExampleV1Client struct {
	restClient rest.Interface
}

// NewForConfig creates a new ExampleV1Client for the given config.
// NewForConfig is equivalent to NewForConfigAndClient(c, httpClient),
// where httpClient was generated with rest.HTTPClientFor(c).
func NewForConfig(c *rest.Config) (*ExampleV1Client, error) {
	config := *c
	if err := setConfigDefaults(&config); err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}
	httpClient, err := rest.HTTPClientFor(&config)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}
	return NewForConfigAndClient(&config, httpClient)
}

// NewForConfigAndClient creates a new ExampleV1Client for the given config and http client.
// Note the http client provided takes precedence over the configured transport values.
func NewForConfigAndClient(c *rest.Config, h *http.Client) (*ExampleV1Client, error) {
	config := *c
	if err := setConfigDefaults(&config); err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}
	client, err := rest.RESTClientForConfigAndClient(&config, h)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}
	return &ExampleV1Client{client}, nil
}

// NewForConfigOrDie creates a new ExampleV1Client for the given config and
// panics if there is an error in the config.
func NewForConfigOrDie(c *rest.Config) *ExampleV1Client {
	client, err := NewForConfig(c)
	if err != nil {
		panic(err)
	}
	return client
}

// New creates a new ExampleV1Client for the given RESTClient.
func New(c rest.Interface) *ExampleV1Client {
	return &ExampleV1Client{c}
}
4. EDIT /workspace/crd_client.go
Before
func setConfigDefaults(config *rest.Config) error {
	config.GroupVersion = &metav1.GroupVersion{Group: "example.com", Version: "v1"}
	config.APIPath = "/apis"
	config.NegotiatedSerializer = rest.CodecFactoryForGeneratedClient(
		runtime.NewScheme(),
		runtime.NewCodecFactory(runtime.NewScheme()),
	).WithoutConversion()

	if config.UserAgent == "" {
		config.UserAgent = rest.DefaultKubernetesUserAgent()
	}

	return nil
}
After
func setConfigDefaults(config *rest.Config) error {
	gv := schema.GroupVersion{Group: "example.com", Version: "v1"}
	config.GroupVersion = &gv
	config.APIPath = "/apis"

	// Create a scheme for the custom resource
	scheme := runtime.NewScheme()

	// Register the types in the scheme
	scheme.AddKnownTypeWithName(gv.WithKind("Widget"), &Widget{})
	scheme.AddKnownTypeWithName(gv.WithKind("WidgetList"), &WidgetList{})

	// Set up the serializer with the scheme
	config.NegotiatedSerializer = rest.CodecFactoryForGeneratedClient(scheme, runtime.NewCodecFactory(scheme)).WithoutConversion()

	if config.UserAgent == "" {
		config.UserAgent = rest.DefaultKubernetesUserAgent()
	}

	return nil
}

// widgets implements WidgetInterface
type widgets struct {
	client    rest.Interface
	namespace string
}

// newWidgets returns a Widgets client for the given namespace
func newWidgets(c *ExampleV1Client, namespace string) *widgets {
	return &widgets{
		client:    c.restClient,
		namespace: namespace,
	}
}

// Create takes the representation of a widget and creates it
// Returns the server's representation of the widget, and an error if there is any
func (w *widgets) Create(ctx context.Context, widget *Widget, opts metav1.CreateOptions) (*Widget, error) {
	result := &Widget{}
	err := w.client.Post().
		Namespace(w.namespace).
		Resource("widgets").
		VersionedParams(&opts, runtime.NewParameterCodec(runtime.NewScheme())).
		Body(widget).
		Do(ctx).
		Into(result)
	return result, err
}

// Get takes name of the widget, and returns the corresponding widget object
// and an error if there is any
func (w *widgets) Get(ctx context.Context, name string, opts metav1.GetOptions) (*Widget, error) {
	result := &Widget{}
	err := w.client.Get().
		Namespace(w.namespace).
		Resource("widgets").
		Name(name).
		VersionedParams(&opts, runtime.NewParameterCodec(runtime.NewScheme())).
		Do(ctx).
		Into(result)
	return result, err
}

// List takes label and field selectors, and returns the list of widgets that match

func (w *widgets) List(ctx context.Context, opts metav1.ListOptions) (*WidgetList, error) {
	result := &WidgetList{}

		Namespace(w.namespace).
		Resource("widgets").
		VersionedParams(&opts, runtime.NewParameterCodec(runtime.NewScheme())).
		Do(ctx).
		Into(result)
	return result, err
}

// widgets implements WidgetInterface
type widgets struct {
	client          rest.Interface
	namespace       string
	parameterCodec  runtime.ParameterCodec
}

// newWidgets returns a Widgets client for the given namespace
func newWidgets(c *ExampleV1Client, namespace string) *widgets {
	// Create a scheme and parameter codec for version negotiation
	scheme := runtime.NewScheme()
	scheme.AddKnownTypeWithName(schema.GroupVersion{Group: "example.com", Version: "v1"}.WithKind("Widget"), &Widget{})
	scheme.AddKnownTypeWithName(schema.GroupVersion{Group: "example.com", Version: "v1"}.WithKind("WidgetList"), &WidgetList{})

	paramCodec := runtime.NewParameterCodec(scheme)

	return &widgets{
		client:         c.restClient,
		namespace:      namespace,
		parameterCodec: paramCodec,
	}
}

// Create takes the representation of a widget and creates it
// Returns the server's representation of the widget, and an error if there is any
func (w *widgets) Create(ctx context.Context, widget *Widget, opts metav1.CreateOptions) (*Widget, error) {
	result := &Widget{}
	err := w.client.Post().
		Namespace(w.namespace).
		Resource("widgets").
		VersionedParams(&opts, w.parameterCodec).
		Body(widget).
		Do(ctx).
		Into(result)
	return result, err
}

// Get takes name of the widget, and returns the corresponding widget object
// and an error if there is any
func (w *widgets) Get(ctx context.Context, name string, opts metav1.GetOptions) (*Widget, error) {
	result := &Widget{}
	err := w.client.Get().
		Namespace(w.namespace).
		Resource("widgets").
		Name(name).
		VersionedParams(&opts, w.parameterCodec).
		Do(ctx).
		Into(result)
	return result, err
}
